referrerpolicy="origin-when-cross-origin" src="https://scontent.fcgk12-1.fna.fbcdn.net/v/t39.30808-6/524733431_4247114618904767_5469941089716530043_n.jpg?stp=dst-jpg_s960x960_tt6&amp;_nc_cat=100&amp;ccb=1-7&amp;_nc_sid=aa7b47&amp;_nc_eui2=AeEAUoHLOxqRy80rgIw6HBKKVu8cYD104RVW7xxgPXThFYWITAOJV_hpqpbFLr8OMjsPiyqpLz1tkqDFi8XxH-EX&amp;_nc_ohc=AalPIxTFebsQ7kNvwH504-0&amp;_nc_oc=AdlyCrHeO2TZC0tGoc1fbXtI8quG7Ynkiq4NmRZTUU7DmneiblgM4TshwP7YXwlIfZM&amp;_nc_zt=23&amp;_nc_ht=scontent.fcgk12-1.fna&amp;_nc_gid=Anwxrr1RnCW4zm5n72lRrw&amp;oh=00_AfaN3AiBm9xLChOcSqbLqBKVlp0xNDks9JbdxIEK9-QAOA&amp;oe=68BEE7AB"></div><div class="x9f619 x1n2onr6 x1ja2u2z x78zum5 xdt5ytf x193iq5w xeuugli x1r8uery x1iyjqo2 xs83m0k x1icxu4v x25sj25 x10b6aqq x1yrsyyn"><div class="x78zum5 xdt5ytf xz62fqu x16ldp7u"><div class="xu06os2 x1ok221b"><span class="x193iq5w xeuugli x13faqbe x1vvkbs x1xmvt09 x1lliihq x1s928wv xhkezso x1gmr53x x1cpjm7i x1fgarty x1943h6x xudqn12 x3x7a5m x6prxxf xvq8zen xo1l8bm xzsf02u x1yc453h" dir="auto"><span class="x1lliihq x6ikm8r x10wlt62 x1n2onr6" style="-moz-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box;">Final verdict: Singapore cowplaymoo have higher ticket/cheaper price payoffs.  There are a lot more diamond card players here since the games give more tickets, there are appreciation stars and moo points that are easy to earn (and unlike the measly 100 points we earn in Indoniesa per 10,000 on one machine, appreciation stars can give a ton, like 18,880 for 15 stars).  Machines require less tokens in general, give more credits, or give more tickets per win.  For example, ticket dome is loaded with tons of 500 rolls and even a few 1000 rolls for 3 tokens per play.  Cyclone is 2 balls per token.  Even over the edge and prize rush is only one token per play here (as opposed to the absurd 4 tokens in Jakarta). The staff are also more lenient with cards: even if there is a bridge and the cards haven't fallen in, the staff will gladly give you the cards.  I have also seen the machines break down more often here in favor of the player, with jackpots activating for no reason.  Personally, I have on video the Premier card button being stuck and the game (Spiderman, which has forced premium drop in Singapore), just spit out all of its contents until there were no cards left.  I paid very few topups under the cheapest option and was able to achieve Platinum quickly unlike in Indonesia.

But here is the catch, the staff is small and absolutely miserable.  I spoke to many staff member at five different CPCM locations and they are worked like slaves with very few people to help.  For example, at the major Suntec location, on a packed Sunday, the line had more than 15 people and there was one register open and was manned by a single kid who only worked a few days, was confused and overwhelmed.  The register is also in charge of converting your cards to tickets and checking set completion, also adding to the waittime.  Machines are often broken and staff members are unwilling to try to debug the machines and will wait until a technician to show up on a different day.  This is the reason why CPCM has so many 1 star reviews in Singapore: the staff is miserable and wait time is forever in every aspect of CPCM.  The prizes are also a lot more limited, the most expensive being worth 200,000 tickets.

Overall, in Singapore verse Indonesia, I still rather play in Singapore because it feels it is cheaper, less frugal, easier to win and that your tickets actually have value.  But my experience in Singapore makes me appreciate the staff in Indonesia more and that they really do make CPCM a lot better.</span></span></div><div class="xu06os2 x1ok221b"><span class="x193iq5w
